<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;"><b>Streamline Health</b>&#174;<b> Reports Fiscal Third Quarter 2024 Financial Results, Accelerates Anticipated Adjusted EBITDA Breakeven Timeline</b></p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">Atlanta, GA, December 16, 2024 (Globe Newswire) &#8211; <b>Streamline Health Solutions, Inc.</b>&nbsp;<b>(</b>&#8220;<b>Streamline</b>&#8221;<b> or the </b>&#8220;<b>Company</b>&#8221;<b>) (Nasdaq: STRM)</b>, a leading provider of solutions that enable healthcare providers to proactively address revenue leakage and improve financial performance, today announced financial results for the third quarter of fiscal 2024, which was the three-month period ended October 31, 2024, and the nine-month period ended October 31, 2024.</p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;"><b>Fiscal Third Quarter and Nine-Months Ended October 31, 2024 GAAP Financial Results</b></p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;"><i>The following financial results have been prepared in accordance with Generally Accepted Accounting Principles (</i>&#8220;<i>GAAP</i>&#8221;<i>).</i></p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">Total revenue for the third quarter of fiscal 2024 was $4.4 million compared to $6.1 million during the third quarter of fiscal 2023. For the nine months ended October 31, 2024, revenue totaled $13.2 million compared to $17.2 million during the same period in fiscal 2023. The change in total revenue was attributable to previously announced client non-renewals offset by successful implementation of new SaaS contracts.</p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">SaaS revenue for the third quarter of fiscal 2024 totaled $2.9 million, 66% of total revenue, compared to SaaS revenue of $3.9 million, 64% of total revenue during the third quarter of fiscal 2023. For the nine months ended October 31, 2024, SaaS revenue totaled $8.7 million, 66% of total revenue, compared to $10.6 million, 62% of total revenue, during the same period of fiscal 2023. As previously reported, the Company had a SaaS contract which did not renew at the end of its 2023 fiscal year.</p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">Net loss for the third quarter of fiscal 2024 totaled ($2.5 million) compared to a net loss of ($11.9 million) during the third quarter of fiscal 2023. For the nine months ended October 31, 2024 net loss totaled ($8.0 million) compared to a net loss of ($17.3 million) during the 2023 period. The third quarter and first nine months of fiscal 2023 included $10.8 million of impairment expenses offset by a $1.2 million and $1.9 million gain, respectively, from valuation adjustments which did not recur during the same periods in fiscal 2024. Net loss during the third quarter and first nine months of fiscal 2024 reflected lower total revenues and higher interest expense offset by reductions in cost of sales, SG&amp;A and R&amp;D expense of $1.9 million and $5.3 million, respectively, primarily due to the Company&#8217;s strategic restructuring at the end of fiscal 2023.</p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<div class="PGBK" style="width: 100%; margin-left: 0pt; margin-right: 0pt">
<div class="PGFTR" style="text-align: center; width: 100%">
<div class="hf-row">
<div class="hf-cell PGNUM">&nbsp;</div>
</div>
</div>

<hr style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always; border: none; width: 100%; height: 2px; color: #000000; background-color: #000000">

<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; margin: 0pt; text-align: left">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">Cash and cash equivalents as of October 31, 2024, were $0.8 million compared to $3.2 million as of January 31, 2024. The Company had no outstanding balance on its revolving credit facility as of October 31, 2024, compared to $1.5 million as of January 31, 2024. Subsequent to the end of the quarter, on November 13, 2024, the Company and its principal lender amended certain financial covenants related to the Company&#8217;s senior term loan and revolving line of credit, which are described in more detail in the Company&#8217;s Quarterly Report on Form 10-Q for the fiscal quarter ended October 31, 2024. On November 20, 2024, the Company received a $1.0 million draw from its revolving line of credit.</p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;"><b>Fiscal Third Quarter and Nine Months Ended October 31, 2024 Non-GAAP Financial Results </b></p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">Adjusted EBITDA for the third quarter of fiscal 2024 was a loss of ($0.3 million) compared to $0.4 million during the third quarter of fiscal 2023. Adjusted EBITDA for the nine months ended October 31, 2024, was a loss of ($1.3 million) compared to a loss of ($1.8 million) during the same period in fiscal 2023. The change in adjusted EBITDA reflects lower total revenue as a result of the previously announced client non-renewals, offset by significant cost savings achieved through the previously announced strategic restructuring.</p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">As of October 31, 2024, the Company&#8217;s total Booked SaaS Annual Contract Value (&#8220;ACV&#8221;) was $14.1 million compared to $15.0 million as of January 31, 2024. $12.0 million of the Booked SaaS ACV was implemented as of October 31, 2024, compared to $11.1 million as of January 31, 2024.</p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">Booked SaaS ACV represents the annualized value of all executed SaaS contracts, including contracts that have not been fully implemented as of the measurement date, assuming any contract that expires during the twelve months following the measurement date is renewed on its existing terms unless the Company has knowledge of the non-renewal.</p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">The Company reiterated that it believes its adjusted EBITDA breakeven run rate is $15.5 million of implemented SaaS ARR and expects to achieve this run rate during the first half of fiscal 2025. Due to the continued unpredictability of timing related to the closing of new contracts, the Company has not provided more specific guidance related to the timing of bookings.</p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;"><b>Management Commentary</b></p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&#8220;During the quarter we expanded existing relationships through our new eValuator quality module, completed implementation for key accounts, including our first enterprise clients and added new logo wins. The resulting momentum has led us to accelerate our expected Adjusted EBITDA breakeven timeline,&#8221; stated Ben Stilwill, President and Chief Executive Officer of the Company. &#8220;The Streamline team is focused on expanding our client footprint, maintaining a high caliber of client service, improving our solutions and progressing our financial goals and our mission to ensure our nation&#8217;s health systems are paid for all of the care they provide.&#8221;</p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;"><b>About Streamline</b></p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">Streamline Health Solutions, Inc.&nbsp;(Nasdaq: STRM) enables healthcare organizations to proactively address revenue leakage and improve financial performance. We deliver integrated solutions, technology-enabled services and analytics that drive compliant revenue leading to improved financial performance across the enterprise. For more information, visit&nbsp;<u>www.streamlinehealth.net</u>.</p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;"><b>Non-GAAP Financial Measures</b></p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">Streamline reports its financial results in accordance with&nbsp;U.S.&nbsp;generally accepted accounting principles (&#8220;GAAP&#8221;). Streamline&#8217;s management also evaluates and makes operating decisions using various other measures. One such measure is adjusted EBITDA, which is a non-GAAP financial measure. Streamline&#8217;s management believes that this measure provides useful supplemental information regarding the performance of Streamline&#8217;s business operations.</p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">Streamline defines&nbsp;&#8220;adjusted EBITDA&#8221;&nbsp;as net earnings (loss) before net interest expense, income tax expense (benefit), depreciation, amortization, share-based compensation expense, valuation adjustments, restructuring charges, transaction related expenses and other expenses that do not relate to our core operations such as severance and impairment charges. A table&nbsp;reconciling&nbsp;this measure&nbsp;to &#8220;net loss,&#8221; to the extent relevant items were recognized in the periods covered,&nbsp;is included in this press release.</p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">Booked SaaS ACV represents the annualized value of all executed SaaS contracts, including contracts that have not been fully implemented, as of the measurement date, assuming any contract that expires during the twelve months following the measurement date is renewed on its existing terms unless the Company has knowledge of the non-renewal.&nbsp;Booked SaaS ACV should be viewed independently of revenue and does not represent revenue calculated in accordance with GAAP on an annualized basis, as it is an operating metric that can be impacted by contract execution start and end dates and renewal rates.&nbsp;Booked SaaS&nbsp;ACV is not intended to be a replacement for, or forecast of, revenue.&nbsp;There is no GAAP measure comparable to Booked SaaS ACV.</p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>
